  805. # [07:01] <@bz> 1) Implement a new MIR instruction for DOM methods, that does all the argument stuff as part of the instruction
  806. # [07:01] * Joins: jduell (jduell@moz-E765EB2E.hsd1.wa.comcast.net)
  807. # [07:01] <@bz> 2) Implement the corresponding LIR instruction
  808. # [07:01] * Quits: ddahl (ddahl@5D3B67E3.71E1659D.DFB5E910.IP) (Input/output error)
  809. # [07:01] <@bz> 3) Change ion codegen for DOM methods to emit those
  810. # [07:02] <@bz> 4) Remove the check I added to keep people from adding no-op [Pure] on methods
  811. # [07:02] <@bz> See also http://pastebin.mozilla.org/2425647
  812. # [07:03] <deian> bz: thanks, taking a look now
  813. # [07:03] <@bz> Basically, the current setup for calls in ion means they're not usefully movable
  814. # [07:03] <@bz> so there is no point marking them as [Pure] in the binding code
  815. # [07:03] <@bz> since ion will just ignore that
  816. # [07:04] <@bz> And the reason they're not movable is that calls are actually two separate MIR instructions
  817. # [07:04] <@bz> MPrepareCall and MCall
  818. # [07:04] <@bz> The former allocates stack space for the arguments (and I think puts them in there)
  819. # [07:04] <@bz> The latter does the call
  820. # [07:04] <deian> aha, gotcha
  821. # [07:04] * @bz never got a good answer for _why_ that's done
  822. # [07:04] <@bz> so the point is you would have to make sure that MCall and MPrepareCall moved together if either one moves
  823. # [07:05] <@bz> and that seems to be rocket science
  824. # [07:05] * Quits: ehugg (ehugg@moz-EA33CD8D.hsd1.wa.comcast.net) (Quit: ehugg)
  825. # [07:05] <@bz> It's easy enough to make sure the MCall doesn't move unless the MPrepareCall moves
  826. # [07:05] * Quits: damons (gnubeard@moz-BCB43F5D.hsd1.ca.comcast.net) (Quit: damons)
  827. # [07:05] <@bz> but the other way around is hard
  828. # [07:05] <philor> what part of https://tbpl.mozilla.org/?tree=Mozilla-Inbound&rev=de1c0246854c could possibly have caused failures in three Android 2.2 reftests, moreso only when rebased since they were green on try in https://tbpl.mozilla.org/?tree=Try&rev=17dcf510b7bb?
  829. # [07:05] <@bz> since the MPrepareCall has no dependency on the later MCall, of course
